PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
No. ll(2),PWO[36( e-l ll2o20.
\ /hereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative sanction that a
total of 1.81.06 heciares of land is required in Thiruvambalapuram village in Radhapuram
Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose, namely, Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar-Nambiyar
lnterlinking Flood carrier canal Project. Environmental lmpact Assessment study for the inigation
pro.iect (ie)formation of Flood carrier canal from Kannadian channel to drought prone Areas of
sattankulam and risayanvillai by lnterlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar Rivers in
Tirunelveli and rhoothukudi Districts in Tamilnadu has been carried out by " M/s. wApcos,'under
section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act '1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation
of Flood carier canal. As the Environment lmpact Assessment study has been carried out
for this irrigation project, social lmpact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of
sub-seclion 2 of section 6 of Right lo Fair compensation and rransparency in Land Acquisition,
Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 2013. The Requisitioning body has not entered upon the
project area and canal was not dug for the Flood carrier project. No family was displaced due
to the land acquisition. The sub collector, cheranmahadevi is appointed as Administrator for the
purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notified that for lhe above said project in
Thiruvambalapuram Mllage of Radhapuram Taluk in Tirunelveli District, land measuring an exlenl of
'1.81.06 heclares, the details of which are specified in the schedule below, is under acquisition:

Resettlement Acl, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern'
A plan of the land may be inspected in the oflices of the Collector and Land Acquisition Officer on any working day during the working hours'
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department Viz., Execulive Engineer, Water Resources Deparlment, Special Project Division, 'llrunelveli
and his staff to enter upon " "r*"vl"nJ,Gt" 
tevets ot an/tand, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work
as provided and specilied in section 12 of the said Act'
under sub-section (4) of seclion 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaclion of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or creale
any encumbrances on such land trom the aate of publication of this Notification in the Tamil Nadu Governmenl Gazette without prior approval of the Collector'
Objections to the acquisilion, if any, may be filed by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this notification in the Tamil
Nadu Government Gazette as provided under section '15 of the said Act before the collector'

PRELIMTNARY NOTIFICATION
No. ll(2)/PwDr36(e-31t202o
Vvhereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total of 50.67.55 hectares of land is required in the Vrjayanarayanam
Environmental impact Assessmenl Study for the irrigiton project (i.e) formation of tlood Carrier Canal from kannadian Channel to drought Prone areas of Sathankulam
and Thisayanvilai by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar rivers in firunelveli and Thoothukudi districts in Tamil Nadu has been carried out by
"M/s. WAPCOS' under the seclion 3(3) of lhe Enviornmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired lo wit for the formation of Flood Carrier Canal. As the
environment impact Assessment Study has been carried out for this irrigation project, Social impact Assessment shall not apply according to the provision of the
sub section 2 of session of 6 of Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Acl 2013. The requisitioning
body did not enler up on the project area on and canal was not dug for Flood Carrier Projecl. No family was displaced due to the land acquisition. The Sub
Collector, Cheranmahadevi is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notilied that for the above said project in
lhe yrjayanarayanam paer-2 Mllage of Thisaiyanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli Oiskict, land measuring an exlenl of 50.67.55 hectares, the details are specified in the

Mllage in Thisayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely Tamirabarani-Karumeniyar -Nambiyar Interlinking Flood Carrier Canal
Project. Environmental lmpact Assessment Study for the irrigation project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier canal from Kannadian Channel to Drought prone Areas of
Sattankulam, Tisayanvillai by interlinking Tamirabarani, Karumeniyar and Nambiyar Rivers in Tirunelveli and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamilnadu has been carried out
by ' M/s. WAPCOS" under lhe section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired to wii for the formation of Flood Carrier Canal . As the
Environment lmpact Assessment study has been carried out for this irrigation project, Social lmpact Assesment shall not apply according to the provision of sub section
2 6f section 6 of Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and Resettlement Act 20'13. The Requisition body did not enter
on the project area and canal was not dugged to Flood Carrier Project. No family was disptaced due to the land acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi
is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore, it is notified that for the above said project in Vijayanarayanam part-2
Village of llsayanvilai Taluk in Tirunelveli District, land measuring an extent of 0.45.37 hectares, the details of which are specified in the Schedule below, is

This Notification is made under sub-section ('l) of Section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and
Rgsettlement Act, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern
.. , ,A plan of. the land-may be inspected in the office of the Collector and Land Acquisition Officer on any working day during the working hours.
and his staff to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acts required for the proper execution of their work
as provided and specified in section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of Section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or create
any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this Notification in lhe Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazetfe without prior approval of the Collector.
Objections to the acquisition, if any, may be filed by lhe person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Notilication in the
Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazette as provided under section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.

PRELIMINARY NOTIFICATION
No.ll(2)/PWDfl 36(e-8)/2020
Whereas it appears that the appropriate Government has given Administrative Sanction that a total of 120.17.4 hectares of land is required in
Moolakaraipatti Mllage in Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District for public purpose namely Tamirabarani -Karumeniyar- Nambiyar interlinking Flood Carrier
Canal Project. Environmental lmpact Assessment Study for the irrigation project (ie)formation of Flood Carrier canal from Kannadian Channel to Drought
prone Areas of Sattankulam, llsayanvillai by interlinking Tamirabarani Karumeniyar Nambiyar Rivers in Tirunelveli and Thoothukudi Districts in Tamil Nadu
has been qarfled out by ""M/s WAPCOS" under the section 3(3) of the Environmental Protection Act 1986. The land is acquired to wit for the formation of
Flood Carrier Canal. As the Environment lmpact Assessment study has been carried out for this irrigation project, Social lmpact Assesment shall not apply
according to the provision of sub section 2 of section 6 of Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabililation and Resetfement
Act 201C The Requisitioning body did not enter on the project area on and canal was not dug for the Flood Carrier Projecl. No family was displaced
due tO the land acquisition. The Sub Collector, Cheranmahadevi is appointed as Administrator for the purpose of Rehabilitation and Resettlement. Therefore,
it is notited thatifor the above said pro.iect in Moolakaraipatii Part-1 Mllage of Nanguneri Taluk in Tirunelveli District, land measuring an exlent ol 0.03.60

. This Notification is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right lo Fair Compensation andTransparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and
Resettlement Act, 2013 (Cenlral Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern
- . A plan.of the land may be inspected in the offlce of the Collector and Land Acquisition Officer on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department (i.e) Executive Engineer, Water Resrouces Department, Special Project Division,
Nanguneri and his staff to enler upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all other acls required for the proper execution
of th;ir work as provided and specilied in section 12 of the said Act. Under sub-section (4) of section 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction
or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, etc or create any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of lhis Notification in the
Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazetfe without prior approval of the Colleclor.
Objections to ihe acquisition, if any, may be filed by the person interested wilhin 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Notification in the
Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazette as provided under section 15 of the said Act before the Collector.

3. Mary Rajan W/o Rajan Suriyadass
489
This Notification is made under sub-section (1) of section 11 of the Right to Fair Compensation and Transparency in Land Acquisition, Rehabilitation and
Resettlement Aci, 2013 (Central Act 30 of 2013), to all whom it may concern.
A plan of the land may be inspdcted in the office of the Collector and Land Acquisition Offlcer on any working day during the working hours.
The Government is pleased to authorize the requisitioning Department Viz.,Executive Engineer, Water Resources Department,Special Project Division, Tirunelveli
and his Staff to enter upon a survey land, take levels of any land, dig or bore into the sub-soil and do all olher acts required for the proper execulion of their work
as provided and specified in section 12 of the said Act.
Under sub-section (4) of seclion 11 of the said Act, no person shall make any transaction or cause any transaction of land (i.e.) sale / purchase, elc or creale
any encumbrances on such land from the date of publication of this Notification in lhe Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazetle wilhout prior approval of the Collector.
Obiections to the acquisition, if any, may be filed by the person interested within 60 (Sixty ) days from the date of publication of this Nolificalion in the
Tamil Nadu Govemment Gazefte as provided under seclion 15 of the said Act before the Collector.
*.ror,roaor,
Principal Secretary to Govemment.
